    add_to_array = {
        global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates = global.date index = 0
    }
}

#宣战
OCF_After_collapse_government_Declare_war = {

    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = {
                    tag = ROOT
                }
            }
            declare_war_on = {
                target = PREV type = annex_everything
            }
        }
    }
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                is_core_of = EIA
                is_core_of = INP
                is_core_of = OFC
                is_core_of = KEZ
                is_core_of = SIE
                is_core_of = FLA
                is_core_of = KCL
                is_core_of = KGF
                is_core_of = ROM
                is_core_of = TKD
                is_core_of = GFZ
                is_core_of = BRI
            }
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
            }
            add_state_core = PREV
        }
    }
}


#内战结束
OCF_end_of_civil_war = {
    OCF = {
        OCF_reset_ruling_party = yes
        OCF_clear_all_deputy_leaders = yes
        set_country_flag = OCF_abolition_parliament_yes_flag
        transfer_state = 115
        add_state_core = 115
        inherit_technology = ROOT
        set_variable = {
            OCF_bill = 150
        }
        country_event = {
            id = OCF.2 days = 4
        }
        load_focus_tree = NO_focus_tree
    }

    ROOT = {
        transfer_navy = {
            target = OCF
        }
    }
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
            NOT = {
                tag = ROOT
            }
        }
        ROOT = {
            annex_country = {
                target = PREV transfer_troops = yes
            }
        }
        every_unit_leader = {
            set_nationality = OCF
        }
    }
    ROOT = {
        every_unit_leader = {
            set_nationality = OCF
        }
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            tag = INP
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
            }
            set_nationality = {
                target_country = OCF
                character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_character = INP_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
            }
            set_nationality = {
                target_country = OCF
                character = INP_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
            }
        }
        OCF = {
            set_cosmetic_tag = INP_unification
            set_politics = {
                ruling_party = fascism
            }
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = fascism
                popularity = 1
            }
            promote_character = {
                character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
                ideology = sub_Regressivism
            }
            promote_character = {
                character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
                ideology = sub_Facism
            }
            add_ideas = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
            annex_country = {
                target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
            }
            change_tag_from = ROOT
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                tag = OFC
                tag = KEZ
                tag = SIE
                tag = KCL
                tag = KGF
                tag = BRI
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                TAG = KEZ
            }
            set_global_flag = OCF_civil_war_so_it_was_unified_flag_KEZ
        }
        OCF = {
            set_cosmetic_tag = OCF_fourth
            annex_country = {
                target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
            }
            change_tag_from = ROOT
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            tag = TKD
        }
        OCF = {
            set_cosmetic_tag = TKD_kingdom
            annex_country = {
                target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
            }
            change_tag_from = ROOT
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            tag = GFZ
        }
        OCF = {
            set_cosmetic_tag = GFZ_unification
            annex_country = {
                target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
            }
            change_tag_from = ROOT
        }
    }
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            has_state_flag = regions_belonging_OCF_flag
        }
        remove_core_of = ANA
        remove_core_of = OFC
        remove_core_of = KEZ
        remove_core_of = SIE
        remove_core_of = FLA
        remove_core_of = KCL
        remove_core_of = KGF
        remove_core_of = ROM
        remove_core_of = TKD
        remove_core_of = GFZ
        remove_core_of = BRI
        remove_core_of = INP
        remove_core_of = EIA
        add_core_of = OCF
        transfer_state = OCF

    }
}

#崩溃的政府体系计算
OCF_collapsed_government_system_yes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system
            add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
            add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
            add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
            add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
            add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
            add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
        }
        remove_ideas = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
    }
    else = {
        add_ideas = OCF_collapsed_government_system_7
    }
}

#近乎为零的政府信誉计算
OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_yes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility
            add_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_1
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_1
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_1
            add_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_2
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_2
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_2
            add_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_3
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_3
        }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_3
            add_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_4
        }
    }
    else = {
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_4
            add_idea = OCF_Almost_zero_government_credibility_5
        }
    }
}

OCF_Random_infrastructure = {
    random_owned_controlled_state = {
        limit = {
            free_building_slots = {
                building = infrastructure
                size > 0
            }
            OR = {
                is_in_home_area = yes
                NOT = {
                    owner = {
                        any_owned_state = {
                            free_building_slots = {
                                building = infrastructure
                                size > 0
                            }
                            is_in_home_area = yes
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        add_building_construction = {
            type = infrastructure
            level = 1
            instant_build = yes
        }
        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
    }
}

#初始化资金调整
set_custom_slider = {
    for_loop_effect = {
        start = 0
        end = 101
        value = val
        add_to_array = {
            slider_buttons = val
        }
    }
    for_loop_effect = {
        start = 0
        end = 101
        value = val
        add_to_array = {
            OCF_adjusting_military_spending_buttons = val
        }
    }
    for_loop_effect = {
        start = 0
        end = 101
        value = val
        add_to_array = {
            OCF_adjusting_education_expenses_buttons = val
        }
    }
    for_loop_effect = {
        start = 0
        end = 101
        value = val
        add_to_array = {
            OCF_adjusting_medical_treatment_buttons = val
        }
    }
}

##资金获取（效果预估）
OCF_obtain_banknotes_effect_estimation = {
    set_variable = {
        tax_impact_effect_estimation = current_int
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact_effect_estimation = -0.1
    }
    #计算修正（抬高税收稳定度修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact_effect_estimation = ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact_effect_estimation = 0.01
    }


    #获取民用工厂
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ROOT.num_of_civilian_factories
    }
    #计算修正（民用工厂税收贡献修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2
    }
    #获取稳定度
    set_variable = {
        OCF_stability_variable_30 = ROOT.stability
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF_stability_variable_30 < 0.3
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_stability_variable_30 = 0.3
        }
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
    }
    #税收基础值
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
    }
    set_variable = {
        tax_impact = current_int
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact = 0.1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = tax_impact
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
    }
    #计算修正（税收修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2
    }
    OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_estimate = yes
    set_variable = {
        OCF_spending_funds_variable = 2
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_war = yes
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
        }
        subtract_from_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
        }
        #获取战争支持
        set_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
        }
        divide_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 800
        }
        #军队花费
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
        }
        #计算修正（军费开支修正）
        set_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
        }
        #计算修正（军费战时开支修正）
        set_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2
        }
        #减去军队花费
    }
    else = {
        set_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
        }
        subtract_from_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
        }
        #获取战争支持
        set_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
        }
        divide_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 2000
        }
        #军队花费
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
        }
        #计算修正（军费开支修正）
        set_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
        }
        #计算修正（军费维护开支修正）
        set_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2
        }
        #减去军队花费
    }
    #军费修正
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_military_spending_int
    }
    set_variable = {
        military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = adjusting_military_spending_int
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = -20
    }
    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = 0.2
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = 0.01
    }
    #教育修正
    set_variable = {
        adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = adjusting_education_expenses_int
    }
    #计算修正（教育开支修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_education_expenses_int_2
    }
    set_variable = {
        education_revision_effect_estimation = adjusting_education_expenses_int
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        education_revision_effect_estimation = 0.2
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        education_revision_effect_estimation = -5
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        education_revision_effect_estimation = 0.01
    }
    #医疗修正
    set_variable = {
        adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2 = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
    }
    #计算修正（医疗开支修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2
    }
    set_variable = {
        medical_correction_effect_estimation = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        medical_correction_effect_estimation = -15
    }
    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        medical_correction_effect_estimation = 0.2
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        medical_correction_effect_estimation = 0.01
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0.1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
    }
    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
    }
    #计算修正（资金总开支修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_expenditure_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2
    }
}

#资金（ 获取资金）
OCF_obtain_banknotes = {
    #获取民用工厂
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ROOT.num_of_civilian_factories
    }
    #计算修正（民用工厂税收贡献修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2
    }


    #获取稳定度
    set_variable = {
        OCF_stability_variable_30 = ROOT.stability
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF_stability_variable_30 < 0.3
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_stability_variable_30 = 0.3
        }
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
    }
    #税收基础值
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
    }

    set_variable = {
        tax_impact = current_int
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact = 0.1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = tax_impact
    }


    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
    }

    #计算修正（税收修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2
    }

    set_variable = {
        tax_impact = current_int
    }
    #显示的稳定度下降
    add_to_variable = {
        tax_impact = 0 #废弃
    }


    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact = -0.1
    }

    #计算修正（抬高税收稳定度修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact = ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2
    }

    set_variable = {
        tax_impact_100 = tax_impact
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        tax_impact_100 = 0.01
    }
    #加成数值
    OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold = yes
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_bill = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable
    }
    if = {
        #AI的每月额外资金
        limit = {
            is_ai = yes
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_bill = 50
        }
    }
    OCF_spending_funds = yes
}


#获取资金阈值（预估）
OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_estimate = {
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = 70
    }
    #计算修正（税收上限修正）
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = modifier@ocf_tax_cap_correction
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable > OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable < 2
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = 2
        }
    }
}

#获取资金阈值
OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold = {
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = 70
    }
    #计算修正（税收上限修正）
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = modifier@ocf_tax_cap_correction
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable > OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable < 2
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = 2
        }
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_bill = modifier@ocf_capital_monthly_additional_funds
    }
}

#花费资金
OCF_spending_funds = {
    set_variable = {
        OCF_spending_funds_variable = 2
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_war = yes
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
        }
        subtract_from_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
        }
        #获取战争支持
        set_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
        }
        divide_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 800
        }
        #军队花费
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
        }

        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
        }

        #计算修正（军费开支修正）
        set_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
        }
        #计算修正（军费战时开支修正）

            ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2
        }
        #减去军队花费
    }
    else = {
        set_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
        }
        subtract_from_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
        }
        #获取战争支持

        }
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
        }
        divide_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 2000
        }
        #军队花费
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
        }

        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
        }



        #计算修正（军费开支修正）
        set_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
        }
        multiply_variable = {

        }
        multiply_variable = {
            OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2
        }
        #减去军队花费
    }
    #军费修正
    set_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_military_spending_int
    }

    set_variable = {

    }
    add_to_variable = {
        military_expenditure_impact = -20
    }
    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        military_expenditure_impact = 0.2
    }
    #加成数值
    set_variable = {
        adjusting_military_spending_int_100 = military_expenditure_impact
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        adjusting_military_spending_int_100 = 0.01
    }
    #加成数值

    #教育修正

    set_variable = {
        adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = adjusting_education_expenses_int
    }

    #计算修正（教育开支修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2
    }


    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_education_expenses_int_2
    }

    set_variable = {
        education_revision = adjusting_education_expenses_int
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        education_revision = 0.2
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        education_revision = -5
    }
    #默认值
    set_variable = {
        education_revision_100 = education_revision
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        education_revision_100 = 0.01
    }
    #加成数值

    #医疗修正
    set_variable = {
        adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2 = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
    }
    #计算修正（医疗开支修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2
    }


    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2
    }

    set_variable = {
        medical_correction = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        medical_correction = -15
    }
    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        medical_correction = 0.2
    }
    #加成数值
    set_variable = {
        medical_correction_100 = medical_correction
    }
    #加成数值
    multiply_variable = {
        medical_correction_100 = 0.01
    }
    #加成数值

    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0.1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
    }
    #默认值
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
    }

    #计算修正（资金总开支修正）
    set_variable = {
        ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = 1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_expenditure_correction
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2
    }


    subtract_from_variable = {
        OCF_bill = OCF_spending_funds_variable
    }
    #每月花费
}

#计算政府影响力
OCF_calculate_government_influence = {
    if = {
        #大洋社会主义同盟
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1 = 8
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_1
        }
    }
    if = {
        #大洋联邦社会联盟党
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_2 = 8
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_2
        }
    }
    if = {
        #改组派民主保全会

            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_3 = 8
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_3
        }
    }
    if = {
        #大洋联邦同盟党
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_4 = 8
        }
        set_variable = {

    }
    if = {

        #玛娜维护协会

#输入变量 pie_chart_angle 角度
#输出变量 coordinate_x x坐标
OCF_calculation_x_position = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pie_chart_angle > 180 } }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { pie_chart_angle = 180 }
        set_temp_variable = { decreased = 1 }
    }

    set_temp_variable = { up_s = pie_chart_angle }
    multiply_temp_variable = { up_s = 7 }
    set_temp_variable = { up_s_2 = 180 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { up_s_2 = pie_chart_angle }
    multiply_temp_variable = { up_s = up_s_2 }

    set_temp_variable = { down_s = 50000 }
    set_temp_variable = { down_s_2 = 180 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle }
    multiply_temp_variable = { down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { down_s = down_s_2 }

    set_temp_variable = { coordinate_x = up_s }
    divide_temp_variable = { coordinate_x = down_s }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { decreased = 1 } }
        multiply_temp_variable = { coordinate_x = -1 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { pie_chart_angle = 180 }
        set_temp_variable = { decreased = 0 }
    }
}

#输入变量 pie_chart_angle 角度
#输出变量 coordinate_y y坐标
OCF_calculation_y_position = {
    set_temp_variable = { angle_init = pie_chart_angle }
    add_to_temp_variable = { pie_chart_angle = 90 }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pie_chart_angle > 180 } }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { pie_chart_angle = 180 }
        set_temp_variable = { decreased = 1 }
    }
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pie_chart_angle > 180 } }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { pie_chart_angle = 180 }
        set_temp_variable = { decreased = 0 }
    }

    set_temp_variable = { up_s = pie_chart_angle }
    multiply_temp_variable = { up_s = 7 }
    set_temp_variable = { up_s_2 = 180 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { up_s_2 = pie_chart_angle }
    multiply_temp_variable = { up_s = up_s_2 }

    set_temp_variable = { down_s = 50000 }
    set_temp_variable = { down_s_2 = 180 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle }
    multiply_temp_variable = { down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { down_s = down_s_2 }

    set_temp_variable = { coordinate_y = up_s }
    divide_temp_variable = { coordinate_y = down_s }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { decreased = 1 } }
        multiply_temp_variable = { coordinate_y = -1 }
        set_temp_variable = { decreased = 0 }
    }
    set_temp_variable = { pie_chart_angle = angle_init }
}

OCF_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correctionresh_national_support_rate = {

#刷新地区支持率
OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = {
    #读取该地区每个党派数量算总数
    set_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
    }

    #保留原数据
    set_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate_100 = THIS.regional_support_rate
    }
    multiply_variable = {
        THIS.regional_support_rate_100 = 0.01
    }

    #计算占比
    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
    }

    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2

        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
    }

    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
    }

    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
    }

    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
    }

    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
    }

    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
    }

    set_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8
    }
    add_to_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
    }

    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }
    divide_variable = {
        THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
    }

    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 }
    set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 }

    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }
    divide_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100 }

    #把数据传入后端， 显示饼图
    OCF = {
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_1 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_2 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_3 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_4 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_5 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_6 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_7 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7
        }
        set_variable = {
            factions_region_8 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8
        }

        #储存真实百分比
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage }
        set_variable = { THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage }
    }

    #计算当前最高值和计算可能胜选党派
    set_variable = {
        THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
    }
    set_variable = {
        THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 1
    }

    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 = 0
    }
    #初始化各个党派
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 = 0
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 2
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 3
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 4
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 5
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 6
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 7
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
        }
        set_variable = {
            THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 8
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 1
            }
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 = 1
        }
    }

    #计算可能胜出党派
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 0
    }
    #胜选派
    set_variable = {
        PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max = 0
    }
    #最大胜选派
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 1
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 2
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 3
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 4
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 5
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 6
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 7
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 8
        }
    }
    OCF_government_authority = yes
}

#临时大选代码
OCF_election_results = {
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_1 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_2 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_3 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_4 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_5 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_6 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_7 = 0
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_8 = 0
    }
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            is_core_of = OCF is_owned_and_controlled_by = OCF
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 1
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 2
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 3
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 4
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 5
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 6
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 7
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 8
            }
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 1
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_1 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 2
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_2 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 3
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_3 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 4
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_4 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 5
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_5 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 6
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_6 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 7
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_7 = 1
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 8
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_8 = 1
            }
        }
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_1
    }
    set_variable = {
        OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 1
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_2 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 2
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_2
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_3 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 3
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_3
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_4 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 4
        }
        set_variable = {
            OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_4
        }
    }
    if = {

                OCF.OCF_election_results_5 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
            }

            OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 5
        }

OCF_suppress_political_parties = {
    OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = yes
    OCF_Prevent_spillage = yes
    OCF = {
        add_stability = -0.05
        add_to_variable = {
            OCF_bill = -10
        }
        OCF_government_authority = yes
    }
}

        }

            THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = -35

#每月支持率提升
OCF_monthly_support_rate_increase_1 = {
    random_state = {
        limit = {
            is_core_of = OCF is_owned_and_controlled_by = OCF
        }
        add_to_variable = {
            THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 10
        }
        add_to_array = {
            global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_change_record_array = 1 index = 0
        }
        OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = yes
    }
    116 = {
        add_to_variable = {
            THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 5

            global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_change_record_array = 1 index = 0

#将增加随机派系支持
OCF_random_region_supports_changes_add = {
    custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_random_region_supports_changes_add_tt
    hidden_effect = {
        random_list = {
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = 20
                }
            }
            1 = {
                add_to_variable = {
                    THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 = 20
                }
            }
        }
    }

}

#刷新所有地区数据
OCF_refresh_all_regional_data = {
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            is_core_of = OCF
        }
        OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = yes
    }
}

#切换党魁
OCF_switching_party_leaders = {
    OCF = {
        set_variable = {
            OCF_party_opened_tab = 1
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF.OCF_show_all_party_leaders = 5
                }
            }
            remove_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
            if = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = 1
                }
                add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
            }
            if = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = 4
                }
                add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
            }
            if = {
                check_variable = {
                    OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = 5
                }
                add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
            }
            set_variable = {
                OCF_party_leader_5_variable = OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v
            }
        }
    }

}

    }
    clear_array = global.OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_array
    if = {
        limit = {

        }
        add_to_array = {

        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = OCF_topic_7024_flag
            }
        }

#清除当前执政党
OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
    }
    if = {
        limit = {

        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
    }

        }
        clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
    }
}

#清除所有副领导人
OCF_clear_all_deputy_leaders = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_idea_parliament
        }
        remove_ideas = OCF_idea_parliament
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Kagami
        }
        remove_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Kagami
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_idea = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
        }
        remove_ideas = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
    }
}

#选举后重置执政党
OCF_reset_ruling_party = {
    OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = yes
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 1
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
        OCF_elected_faction_1 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 2
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
        OCF_elected_faction_2 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 3
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
        OCF_elected_faction_3 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 4
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
        OCF_elected_faction_4 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 5
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
        OCF_elected_faction_5 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 6
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
        OCF_elected_faction_6 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 7
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
        OCF_elected_faction_7 = yes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 8
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
        OCF_elected_faction_8 = yes
    }
    OCF_party_relations_refresh = yes
}

    set_variable = { OCF_SAMPLE_TIME = global.date }

    set_variable = { OCF_SAMPLE_y_position_1 = OCF_national_support_1_proportion }
    set_variable = { OCF_SAMPLE_last_y_position_2 = OCF_SAMPLE_y_position_2 }

    set_variable = { OCF_SAMPLE_y_position_8 = OCF_national_support_8_proportion }
    if = {
        limit = {

        }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_1 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_1_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_2 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_2_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_3 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_3_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_4 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_4_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_5 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_5_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_6 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_6_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_7 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_7_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_8 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_8_frame index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_SAMPLE_numbers index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_SAMPLE_TIMEs index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_1 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_2 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_3 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_4 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_5 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_6 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_7 index = 0 }
        remove_from_array = { array = OCF_Historical_support_ranking_8 index = 0 }
    }

    set_temp_variable = { OCF_offset_1 = OCF_SAMPLE_last_y_position_1 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { OCF_offset_1 = -1 }
    add_to_array = { global.OCF_historical_parliament_segmentation_1 = OCF_offset_1 }

    set_temp_variable = { OCF_offset_2 = OCF_SAMPLE_last_y_position_2 }
